Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments for fear, because it is necessary to avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the way to work it is that you instruct the patient to knead the intestine with his hand inside the wound, if he can enter it;  
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then have him lean back on his neck between your hands and lift his thighs; 
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then stretch the heart above, and peel all the skin of the buttocks along its length;  
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert wedges of wood into the spaces of the waist according to what you need to open the wound, and let them be such that your eyes can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then flay the skin that is under the leather of the testicles, so that the white firm flesh is uncovered on all sides; 
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then put your index finger into that which follows the testicle, in that which is between the white flesh that is under the skin of the testicle, and between the second flesh, and separate that which is behind the testicle, and between the second flesh. 
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And then move with your right hand inside the heart of the testicles, and stretch the white flesh upward with your left hand, and lift the testicle up away from all the flesh towards the waist. 
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	And instruct the assistant to extend the testicle upward, and loosen that which is behind the ligature.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	And inquire with your fingers if there is any intestine entangled or white firm flesh, and if you find nothing, then put it back into the abdomen below. 
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with a thick thread made of ten threads, and insert it into the back part of the thigh, which is after the skin of the testicles; 
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After the waist, then cut the hairs that appear from the threads, as long as there are four threads; 
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then assemble them one on top of the other in the shape of a cross, and bind the thigh, which we said is below the skin of the testicles, with a strong ligature in two parts; 
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the hairs of the threads and tie them in two parts so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter, so that no abscess may come. 
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	And place a second ligature according to the first ligature, long two fingers from it, and after these two ligatures leave the thigh which is below the heart of the testicles, a finger in width. 
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and afterward all the others according to the roundness which the egg bears; 
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then carve into the part that is under the skin of the testicles, as long as it does not cut the veins and the bowel, as we have said before; 
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply wool softened in oil, and put it on the wounds, and I apply the bandage that we have said. 
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And never cauterize white flesh as we have said after incision, for fear of the shedding of blood.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens many times, and leave the bandage as long as it oozes through it;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it is slow to drain, then it should be washed with hot water, and put on what we have said as long as it oozes; 
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.  
de hernie carnouse	Of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch I have never seen anyone who dared to make the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like a twig that is together with the vine, in part so that you tie the vessels, after cutting under lightly below; 
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut into me, and cure the abscess of the one who works, as long as the vessels weep; 
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And cure it as we have said, until it is healed. 
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes a rupture comes in the angles, as we have said, and open its sides;  
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	And do not draw out any of the intestines at the hips, and if any are drawn out, it is bad, and repair them every hour;  
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	And in all ways if it remains too long in this place, the wound or fistula will grow as long as the intestines are drawn out; 
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens by the extension of the fistula which is at the angles, as we have said, because it is extended, then softened and swells the sides and opens. 
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And the cure is by cautery, as we have said before; 
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And it is sometimes cured with iron in this way: 
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	And have the patient lie often on his back between your hands, then cover the area of the fracture swollen twice as wide according to the quantity of three fingers; 
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	Then extract the sinew which is under the skin than the usual, then take a knife and put it on the apparent area of the sinew. 
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And press at the bottom of the belly, then sew the two apparent areas of the sinew on the head of the knife and sew one and the other.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then extract the head of the knife, and do not cover the sinew nor extend anything else as I have told you in the cure of the rupture of the intestines. 
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then cure it by curing the wounds. 
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, if the patient cleans and cares for the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The sinew is constricted and has no appearance in the fracture, and the cauteries are milder in this place, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Often the skin of the testicles is softened in some men because the membranes inside are softened and it is made to be seen.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary, when one wants to heal it, that one makes the patient lie on his back, and peels off the softened skin from the natural skin. 
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then bring the two lips together with a suture, and if you see fit, sew the excess of the softened skin at three or four sutures firmly. 
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then peel between the sutures, and treat the wound like other wounds, until it is healed, and remove the thread. 
dou chastrement	where cautery
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is forbidden in our law, and therefore it would please me not to speak of it in this book. 
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	And it is only necessary for two reasons.
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	One is that the patient can answer when asked and understands the treatment.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	The other is because we often need to castrate certain beasts to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.  
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that cautery is done according to two manners: 
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by attraction or by incision. 
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In that which we do by attraction, we make the iron sit in sharp heat until the coals are softened and hang down.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then we take them with our hand as long as they are cooled down and you no longer feel them. 
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the cautery of the waist:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	it is necessary that you hold the iron and press the skin of the coals with your left hand, then tie the suspensory, and apply one blow to each eye when you have well scorched them. 
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave no spot so that it can be seen and the subtle spot which is on the vessels.
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this manner of cautery is better than that which is done by attraction because in attraction some coals may remain by chance, which causes the iron to desire luxury.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed. 
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways like men: 
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One is when between the two testicles appears also as the shape of a woman's nature, or he has hair, and sometimes urinates in front. 
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other way is for women, and it has a handle like a rod and two prongs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment of the man and woman is that you cut off all the added flesh, and treat it like other wounds; 
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, men whose urine comes out through the skin of the testicles have no cure.
de la tentigene	From the tentorium
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A tentingene is an added flesh upon the natural part, so long as it is too ugly to see.
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have them as large as a hand, and this is the cure. 
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It behoves you to hold the superfluity of the tentingene in your hand or with forceps, and cut it lightly. 
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not apply too much force, so that blood does not flow, then treat it with another treatment until it is healed. 
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and there is another flesh that grows at the mouth of the wound and spreads, and by chance jumps further, and it appears like a cow, and for this reason the ancients called it the "cow disease." 
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	It is necessary that you cut it as we have said about the tendon, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	Of wandering
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic when the nature of the woman is not perceived, or when the opening is small; 
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or accidental through a sickness that has come;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is by added flesh, or through subtle syphilis or some such thing, and it is made forcefully in the wound, or on the side, or below, or wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and it prevents conception, and childbirth, and by chance having flowers; 
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	And the recognition of these is by looking at the swelling. 
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the splinters are close together, appearing on both sides or to the right.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is a subtle synovial fluid, and it is close to two liters, if you hurry, then do this:  
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Put your two index fingers together, and the woman should be on her back, spread her legs; 
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then extend the two liters, as long as the subtle synovial fluid is gone, and the strainings are over;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, and moisten it in oil, and put it on the spot, and let the woman rest at home each day, so that she cannot sew. 
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syphilis sore is hard and thick, it is fitting that you cut it with a spatula resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the strainings are of bone, suspend it with an onctment and a cop;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and take medicinal substances that staunch blood, such as alum, dragon's blood, frankincense, together with plenty of egg white.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then apply a broad bandage soaked in water so the wound cannot close. 
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And do this for a long time, and apply a tent of dry linen. 
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then it should be treated with other remedies until it is healed. 
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when a boil comes to the flesh, if it should be covered according to this manner, unless it is an ulcerated abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an inflamed abscess which is in the marrow, one must not apply fire.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins which do not usually bleed, and when hemorrhoids are old they become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have said in the division the likenesses of others, and the signs, and I will say here those which receive a cure.  
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and the lul, when they are steeped in marrow, and they do not appear to the feeling, unless it is not cured by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the marsh, one can feel, are those that one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, it is necessary that you place the woman in a cold house, then hold the hemorrhoid with forceps and cut off its stem, then sprinkle medicinal powders that restrain blood, such as alum and dragon's blood and frankincense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then place her feet against the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water. 
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if a discharge of blood comes, let him sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and gallnuts and similar things; then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and oil, and make a plaster on his back. 
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it extinguishes, it is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, let him have cupping on his back and breasts without pricking. 
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take wool and moisten it in plantain juice or elderberry juice with old wine, and apply it to the place. 
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess subsides, treat the area with ointment until it is healed; 
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albather" is red and is similar to sharp alum; if it is needed, cover it as I have said for the thelul; 
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat it until it is healed.  
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses of the cheek
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscess come to the cheek, such as sore and pierced abscess and herpes and inflammations and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have said in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is necessary therefore that I say in this treatise the hot abscess which comes in the marsh, which is not of the abscesses that collect pus; 
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the work of iron, see if the abscess is sharp at the beginning of its arrival, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red when you can see it. 
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but let it mature until the pain is eased; 
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a stool, and let it have two small stools where he leans, and support himself on his back and bring his feet together towards the outer part of the leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his thighs be spread, and put his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good bandage; 
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then draw the abscess towards the right side and prepare the instrument with which one works the mouth of the abscess, from which the shape will come afterward;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you see this instrument being used, you insert the point first to know the depth of the wound, so that what enters the instrument does not go in deeper than it should and so that it does not injure the patient. 
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	And if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths so that the instrument does not injure it. 
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	And it is necessary for him to put the funnel of the instrument above and to hold the instrument.  
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens, and it is made soft with the hand, if necessary cover it at first with linen or a spatula.  
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	And when the bowels are emptied, it is necessary that you put softened tents into the wound in oil of roses, or in dried green oil. 
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and put the strong tent of the wound to the end of the marrow, and put by fire on the marrow and on the handle leave clean linen moistened in vinegar or honey are cooked; 
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then the cure after two days of anointing following it, until it is healed; 
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and no time lift the marrow and the wound by enema of vinegar and honey, and then of vinegar or long roots of lily and aristolochia are cooked; 
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to anointing. 
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is healed in the marsh, it is fitting that you guard against cauterizing with iron, but treat it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	From childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the figure of natural childbirth, and the signs if it is when you see the woman hasten down, and desire to smell the air: 
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child hastens out with force.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then know that those childbirths are according to natural figure, and is the issue under its head, and the afterbirth with it; 
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, it is fitting to press their belly lightly so that the infant comes out quickly; 
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it descends onto its head, the placenta comes with it, and the mother is cleansed of its superfluities by good purification; 
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and this which comes otherwise does not come naturally. 
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it sometimes comes onto its feet, and the body or head comes out first, and the hands, or it comes onto its stomach, or often, and is accidentally turned on its neck, and by other bad positions; 
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in these matters, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the positions how one should help her. 
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the infant comes onto its head by natural passage, and the woman labors painfully, and her strength is weak, then have her sit on a stool, or have women hold her; 
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and make a poultice of oil or fenugreek when cooked, and then insert the ball between its two halves the small spatula which is in this form: 
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the second finger, and cut off at its nail until the moisture that is inside comes out. 
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the belly of the woman until the infant descends, and if it does not descend, then give the woman an enema of fenugreek mucilage with sesame oil. 
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her take and sneeze from mustard seed, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	then the infant will now come out. 
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands come out weak, then you must gently reset them little by little.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, then place the woman on a stool and raise her feet. 
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	Then unseat her from the stool onto the ground, and hold her so she does not shriek during the unseating. 
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if her hands cannot enter, and the child is dead, then cut her hands with a knife that was previously placed there, and extract the child, and reset it equally. 
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the issue of the child upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes onto its feet, if he needs to be pushed upward; 
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is equal.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then take it by the feet and extend it little by little. 
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	If it jumps up to the thighs, then command her to take it and make her sneeze forcefully;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it jumps further, then God wills it. 
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it is not as we have said, if it returns little by little, until it is according to the natural form.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it is light.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come further as we have said, take a mixture of elderflower and sesame oil and melted gum, and grind everything in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put it on the nature of the woman inside and remove this ointment, then make her sit in a warm bath up to under her ribs; 
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is softened underneath, give her a collar of myrrh, and put it underneath, and leave it for an hour; 
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make her sit on a stool, then make her sneeze and draw out her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child leaps now. 
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	from the issue of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this manner, if it puts its hands on its belly little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let it be swaddled on its neck, and hang its feet down, and let it lie upon the bed; 
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold its hands little by little, and then place its hands upon its belly, and remove the cushions underneath until it is fully exposed downwards; 
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, then he takes his feet and lifts them up, then lifts his belly upwards, then pushes with his hands. 
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	And he shakes the child little by little.  
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	And he instructs the woman to hold on until the child sits up. 
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the issue of a child who comes forth, with one hand pendant
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to engineer a way to bring back the hand:  
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If one cannot bring it back, then have the woman stand up and walk. 
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then have her sit on the bed and straighten out her legs.  
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then apply the muscle relaxant that I have described. 
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if she does not give birth, then have her sit on a chair and then study how to bring back the hand.  
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	And shake the child according to its natural form and make it sneeze, instructing her to hold on until the child sits up firmly. 
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the issue of the child upon its neck, and let it spread its hands, and its face turned towards its mother's back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is fitting that the bailiff hold his hand, then turn it little by little, and lift it lightly; 
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is equal, he puts on the natural ointment of ivy and oil, as we have said, then instructs her to move little by little; 
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on a seat, and instruct her to take hold; 
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze. 
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same manner for all the second joints
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes strong in this manner to the entire second joint, he applies the second joint to your fingernail, as long as the moisture is drained; 
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child can put its hands on its face and neck, he applies it from the elbow down so that it is not held back, and kills the child; 
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside as long as you have put it as it should be, and instruct the woman to take hold at no time: 
adonques si istra legierement.	then if you gently pull it 
de l’issue des gemelz	from the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are born many times, and rarely are three or four born; 
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it does happen. 
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are a strange thing, and do not live if born;  
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that when they are multiplied, and are nourished by the milk which flows from the breast;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they are also born naturally as one under another, as we have said. 
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are born prematurely, so the care is as we have said, and the child is delicate, make quickly and gently what she does;  
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do as is best for its salvation. 
de plusors enfans	of several children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb one or two or three or four or five or six or seven, or more up to fifteen, and are all formed in the shape of a child by the measure of the glorious sage, and it is fitting that the midwife knows all this, because such things may happen by chance;  
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	If you do according to what is right. 
de l’enfant mort	Of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman for stillbirth or dead child in the womb, as I have said in the section, and it does not come out, and you are forced to use your hands. 
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	It is necessary that you know if the woman is of sound constitution and has no illness or fear of death.  
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	The woman should be placed on her back, with her hips inclined downwards, and her legs raised. 
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And the attendant should hold her down in two places, or tie her to the bed so that she does not move during the removal of the child. 
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the womb with warm oil mixed with marshmallow and fenugreek mucilage and flaxseed, then anoint her hands with these oils and mucilages. 
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then put them in the marrow slightly, then want the place where they put the splints that are suitable for it, and take care if the child is frightened that he should descend on his head. 
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If he puts the splints in his eyes or in his neck or in his mouth or in his palate or under his beard or in his throat or near his ribs, and if his descent is on foot, then he puts them or a dagger and at the middle ribs. 
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary that he holds the splint in his right hand and puts the curve between the two fingers of his left hand and puts it gently with all his hand and puts the splint in none of these places that we have said, as long as he comes to the empty thing.  
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the splint: 
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then put it against the other splint, or the third if you need it, so that the extraction is equal.  
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they are stretched equally by moving back and forth, in order to come out, and let the incisors be toothed in order to hold them, as this is the form: 
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part remains, anoint the wound with some of its two drops of oil, and put them in that part, and pull out the other part; 
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if none remains, put this incisor or higher up, and do this as much as it comes out all the way. 
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot bring it back because of the tightness, it is fitting that you wrap it up on a cloth, until it comes out all the way; 
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then cut at the joint of the sole or at the knife, and so it is fitting that you do this in the other hand, and with both feet. 
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is stuck in the birth canal, or if there is sharp bone assembled, then you should put the sharp spatula between your fingers, press the head and extract the sharp bone. 
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Then you will turn it to an instrument that is called "almidach," from which the shape comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one. 
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And in the same way, do this if the infant has a large head naturally. 
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	Then pull the bones with tongs, and if the head comes out too far and is extracted by force, it should be split, so that the moisture that is or in the bad birth canal comes out. 
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot come out, then cut it into as many pieces as you can.  
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, then you should pierce it so that the moisture runs out. 
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, the attraction is light, and straightening at the mouth of the uterus is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is embedded in the belly or breast, you should remove it wrapped in a cloth on the hand; 
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and covering the belly or breast, until the moisture which is there runs off;  
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other members are removed, and the head remains, then put the hand on the mouth of the wound and draw it up to the mouth of the wound; 
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then he puts in one or two fingers and draws them out.  
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the mouth of the wound is constricted by a hot boil which has come there, then one should not work at it, but rather administer moist and fatty things;  
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply poultices, made of herbs that are sharp, softening and moistening. 
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the arrow is on its side, and you can put it straight, then administer what we have said about the living child; 
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if one does not have power, so let it be cut into pieces and leave nothing of the sinew. 
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply what we have said about abscesses which come in the marrow.  
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if bleeding comes forth, it should be put into a tight bandage, and apply other treatments. 
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose belly had a dead child inside, then she conceived another on top of it, and the other one was born dead too.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess appeared on his arm, and it swelled so much that it opened, and then began to discharge profusely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat him, and I thought for a long time, and could not sew the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on a plaster of strong attraction, and one bone came out, and after a few days another.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marvelled greatly, for this belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	If I thought they were bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I cleansed the wound and set the bones by hand until the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and I kept the woman for a long time like this, and there remained afterward only a little hump on the spot. 
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have not recorded this chapter other than for this reason: so that when masters encounter a strange thing they may know how to help it. 
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To return the marrow to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here follows the form of the pressor, with which one crushes books;  
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns as the head of the two linens. 
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horn should be more delicate than the restrictor, and should be made of ebony or boxwood. 
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And its mouth should be two fingers wide, and the margin of the trees should be one, and a half palms long. 
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And between the two limbs there should be two adjustments of this same wood, which should be firm on one side and the other, half a palm long or a finger more.  
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two adjustments are fitted into the mouth of the mallet to open when one turns the two horns. 
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more delicate and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the appearance of tongs. 
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	And it has two horns and two adjustments, as you see, a palm long and two fingers wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the vulva open to all instruments, make the woman sit down off the bed with her feet dangling and legs open, then insert the two stirrups together into the vulva, and hold the head of the instrument below between her thighs; 
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on all the instrument, just as you did with the forceps equally, according to the amount that you see the mouth of the vulva open, as long as the woman does what she wants. 
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all mounted and are multiplied in their likenesses;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the surgeon has them prepared, so much quicker is the work, and higher are the hopes for their quantity. 
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not prepare your instruments, their necessity is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second stage is retained in childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze on purpose, and extract your hands from her mouth and nose; 
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she jumps through it, all is well. 
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If it does not, then take a pot and make a hole or lid in it, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the wound, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia lignea and centaury; 
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in a pot with water over the fire; 
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then put a cane or tube in the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the wound, and let it steam until the vapors enter the wound; 
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said. 
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the shoulder jumps quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment and is not healed, order the patient to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or marshmallow mucilage, and then put it on the wound, and let it stay for a while.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she has found it, if she takes hold of it and extends it little by little straight so that the marrow does not break during extraction. 
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But then it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled. 
si venra et se desaerdra.	It will come out and loosen.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the marrow is narrow, we have said the cure is sneezing and fumigating herbs; 
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it's not from all that we have said, be careful not to pull the opposite way; 
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is at the mouth of the marrow tie it to the thigh of the woman, then anoint her with tetrapharmacy ointment. 
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If she purges and returns, and will come out strong;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But in any case, when she purges, it comes with a bad odor to the stomach and head, and weakens the patient. 
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	So it is necessary then suitable fumigations for this: 
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the ancients have experienced fumigation of cress and dried figs.  
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one smokes the woman for the retention of flowers and the afterbirth is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is seen to resemble a cane, and one puts the subtle head in the nature, and the heads wide on the fire; 
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigations be on the coals, and the moth as long as it is eaten up, and begin another. 
de percier lou fondement	To pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but rather have it stopped by a subtle tool: 
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	so it is necessary then for the midwife to pierce that tool with her finger, and not pierce it with a sharp spatula, and she guards the placement so that it does not touch;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on linen moistened in wine and oil, then the cure of anointing until it is healed. 
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will stay in place, put or insert a cane of plum wood, and leave it for seven days, and have it removed when the child wants to go to the chamber pot.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this inflammation comes from the opening of a wound or abscess. 
si covient coper celui soudement:	So it is necessary to cover that opening. 
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	If it is cured, as we have said of the chain of lead. 
de la fistule dou fondement	Of the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come below the buttocks are nodules and swellings that come from below the buttocks or in the space between the two parts, whether it is one fistula or several. 
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that nodule is old, if it works, and still produces moisture which causes white or subtle boils, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by the fact that there is discharge or flatulence when the patient makes a bowel movement, and perhaps it jumps one time. 
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that pierce as far as the bladder and as far as half of the penis; 
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they reach up to the hip joint, and up to the knee. 
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a fistula draining at the fundament, and not draining: 
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you put your thumb or finger on the fundament, and insert a fine needle of silver or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting. 
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has twisting, you put in a tent of fine linen, or a horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair with your finger;  
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there comes no discharge of pus or wind or worm, as we have said: 
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not pierce through;  
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to cure it.  
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends to the bladder or to the urethra, then the urine escapes and cannot be held back by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced up to the hip joint, the tent comes up to that place; 
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no crookedness and the origin of the pain is elsewhere, it is as if he bows to it, and neither medicine nor ointment is of any use.  
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these fistulas that persist there is no stronger cure than hard work, and the vanity of foolish doctors who interfere with it. 
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not persistent and is not old, there is hope of healing with iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back; 
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and he lifts his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of iron, or of lead if there is crookedness, as far as you know where the tent comes. 
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the base, it is fitting that you insert your index finger, and feel then if the tent has pierced it;  
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and let it be uncovered where you feel between your finger the sinew or the flesh, then know that it is pierced. 
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If it does not work, one cannot heal it. 
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One always says that one can heal them well, but this rarely happens;  
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the help that one does, if it is heated according to the width of the fistula as it is said before; 
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and the end all hot in the fistula, as long as it comes from the bottom; 
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this II or III times, as long as you know that these bad sinews are burned, which resemble a bird's feather;  
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the dressing of softened tents in butter, as long as the sinew dries out, then the dressing of ointment hardening sinew and soldering. 
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healed, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this cannot otherwise be healed; 
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent enters but does not pierce through to the bone which is its foundation, and between your finger and the tent there is a thick covering of flesh or sinew, and you see the fistula at that point where it goes beneath this covering. 
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the opening of the fistula is at the beginning and extends forward before the tent, then apply the cautery afterwards, as far as it reaches the head of the tent; 
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent will be delivered and will fall away; 
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then cleanse those faulty flesh parts which resemble a bird's feather, so that none remain. 
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood comes, and is cut between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For fire cauteries bring together two things:  
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	namely, the burning of those added flesh parts, and the stemming of blood and drying of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then apply a dressing softened with butter or crushed cheese until the wound swells, and let the charring be burned in the swelling. 
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with bandages soaked in strong vinegar, which are dry medicines. 
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes all the way to the foundation and is distant from the body, stick it with your thumb or finger, and inquire about this.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the dressing and between the two is cloth or linen or charring, where it is about to pierce, unless there is a way of faith and hope, by the administration of one of the three methods: 
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it to the bottom, or if you can, you put dressings and treat as before. 
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too far in perfection, lest you cut the ligament that holds the foundation, and let the excrement come out against your will;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then treat it as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	Perhaps it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it once it is cut away from the foundation, either by hand or with another pointed instrument. 
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse that rotten flesh which is in the wound, as much as you can. 
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to restore the wound and to keep the fistula on the side away from the foundation.  
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it were a lighter thing for the patient. 
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And fistulas are never made in this manner: 
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and when you insert the tent into the fistula and it is near or touches the foundation of the skin above, then take a pierced tent at its head according to this form. 
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I bend the thread in two, and I put the tent on the whole thread into the fistula as far as the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pierced in the margin of the foundation within, then remove the thread from that perforation, so that you insert your finger or foundation. 
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and treat the head of the thread, and bring together the two ends, and pull one from the other, and leave it for one or two days; 
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it several times, as long as the threads hold those fibers that are between them, and they shrink;  
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is sewn and healed. 
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce, make it pierce in all the ways that you can, as long as it is not too inflamed.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not right to make for the placement cover so soon, and then the cure, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spatuila used for making a fistula must be very sharp and cutting on one side; 
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side, blunt, so that you do not cut what you should not cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Hemorrhoids are according to two manners: 
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	where they are inside the fundament, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they often bleed, and there is one or several, and they protrude from the fundament and at the head of the fundament; 
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those which are weak have a bit of moisture, and still now or a bit of sharp citrine or a bit of blood, and they have the color of the body; 
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment of those who have them in their foundations, if it is such that you command the patient to stretch himself out to go into chambers, until the foundation allows them to appear, and the threads are seen; 
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, and hold it with tweezers, or hold it at your fingernail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the tweezers cannot hold them because of their moisture, then take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of chamois leather; 
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out at your will, then cut them, and powder over them some hot powders that are in place of a cautery; 
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Where you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter of cautery, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed. 
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundations cannot come out, give the patient a harsh and sharp enema to wash out what is in the foundation so that it can come out openly. 
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient complains, and if the thread is strong from the foundation, then the treatment is easy.  
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you take them with your fingernail or with tongs and cut them, then treat them as we have said until they are healed, and that he fears the incision by iron.  
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is fitting that you administer the suture according to this manner: 
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread and put it into a needle, then draw the thread over and make the needle pierce through the other side, then turn both ends of the thread under the needle, and so it is doubled.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and pull out the forming thread, then tie the thread, and pull out the needle, and do so for all the others, and leave it to correct the excess of blood. 
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then put on the base a soft cloth moistened in rose oil or wax, and put it on the base, and instruct the patient to rest. 
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then leave it until they fall out, and when they have fallen out, then cure them with ointment and other cures, until they are healed. 
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	of dryness of the veins or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there occurs dryness of veins in the intestine, and by constriction of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine is of no avail.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you scrape off the bark with the tip of a knife or your fingernail, so as not to let it become moist. 
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then cure it until it is healed as is fitting.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot heal, then start the scraping again stronger than before, until it heals a lot and is well scraped.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal it until it is healthy. 
dou fremit	Where it trembles
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A boil is a small foul appearance against the body, and it goes out very quickly
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and often one finds it cold, and one also feels it as dead numbness, and it comes throughout the body, and more in the hands than anywhere else. 
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure is that you take a cane from a goose quill, or a strong vulture quill, and place that cane on the numbness, until the circles completely encircle the numbness;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand on all of the cane until you grasp it all around the numbness, and pull it out quickly, and uproot the numbness from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see it, make one of a thread of linen or iron according to this form, and let it be thin underneath and wide above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce, but hold tight to the pain and press. 
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see that it must be cauterized, do so as described in the chapter on cautery.  
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a clyster of silver or artichoke is made, or melted lead or mallet; 
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And sometimes these small and large instruments are made, according to those to whom they are administered. 
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore those who are treated in the care of children and who are weak and painful are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large clyster is wide on top, where the belly is tied according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if you see that the belly is tied and pierced as it is, 
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and there are two openings on one side, and one on the other;  
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and the belly or where medicines are placed is made from a bladder of an animal or parchment, and pierced all around with small holes, and there is one space between each hole, then insert into these holes one strong thread of raw silk twisted in X or any shape around them, and assemble the belly as if it were a goat;  
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then give an enema. 
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And this is the shape of the circle: 
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine be neither too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the clyster with oil or yolk of egg, or something similar, then insert it gently. 
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister squeezes it with both hands together until all is squeezed out, then extracts the clyster and has the patient lift their legs to the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, they should hold it as long as they can. 
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if he sleeps all night, it is of greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cauterize it for a disease of flux of the belly, and the medicine hastens to go in, then begin again until it is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the fundament or abscess, let the clyster be as subtle as for a child. 
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the shape of the subtle clyster on which the skin is removed: 
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have said in the aforementioned section the treatment of wounds; 
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we will tell you the treatments with hands and medicine, according to its accomplishment. 
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places or the wounds where they are made, and of what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by the striking of a stone and the cutting of a sword and knife or lance or gun or arrow or similar things;
